MODEL: claude-3-opus-20240229

USER-PROMPT:
Assistant is a Careful and Predictable Step by Step Instruction Template Format Following MODE Today.

You will be solving a string replacement logical puzzle where you apply transformations to a List of Tokens to get New List of Tokens until the Rules no longer creates a New Unique List.

Tokens
- "A#"
- "#A"
- "#B"
- "B#"

Tokens with Numbers Example
- "A#(10)"
- "#A(3)"
- "#B(2)"
- "B#(12)"

NOTE: ONLY Respond with VALID Tokens

# Rules:
RULE:A# #A →
RULE:A# #B → #B A#
RULE:B# #A → #A B#
RULE:B# #B →
RULE:#A #A → #A
RULE:#A A# → #A
RULE:#A B# → #A
RULE:#A #B → #A
RULE:A# A# → A#
RULE:A# B# → A#
RULE:B# A# → B#
RULE:B# B# → B#
RULE:#B #A → #B
RULE:#B A# → #B
RULE:#B B# → #B
RULE:#B #B → #B
RULE:#B → #B
RULE:#A → #A
RULE:A# → A#
RULE:A# → A#

NOTE:
RULE:B# #B →
RULE:A# #A →
Is literally NOTHING not even a Space

OLD TOKENS -> NEW TOKENS

Guide For EVERY STEP
# PASS Guide
1. This is where you take Pairs of Tokens and Copy the Rule Basically
2. For rules:
RULE:A# #A → NOTHING
NEXT INDEX:+2
RULE:A# #B → #B A#
NEXT INDEX:+2
RULE:B# #A → #A B#
NEXT INDEX:+2
RULE:B# #B → NOTHING
NEXT INDEX:+2
RULE:EVERY OTHER RULE -> FIRST TOKEN
NEXT INDEX:+1


# GATHER NEW TOKENS Guide
1. This is Where you Get the New Tokens. Basically Everything After →.
2. Be SURE to Ignore the NOTHING Meaning Literally NOTHING
3. Remember to Keep TWO Separate Counts for the the OLD TOKEN and the NEW TOKENs starting from 1 Known as "OLD COUNT" and "NEW COUNT"
4. AGAIN ALWAYS Start the Count from 1 for OLD TOKENs and NEW TOKENs



# EXACT SAME STRING PREV Guide
1. This is Where Check if the String is the Same so you can just go to "# Tokens Without Numbers" then Submit your Solution inside of <solution></solution>
2. Compare the Two Previous # GATHER NEW TOKENS to Make COMPLETELY SURE They are EXACTLY the SAME



<EXAMPLE 1>
<problem>#A B# #B #B #B #A A# B# #B A# #A #B</problem>

# List Out
1. #A
2. B#
3. #B
4. #B
5. #B
6. #A
7. A#
8. B#
9. #B
10. A#
11. #A
12. #B



# NEW TOKENS:
#A(1) B#(2) #B(3) #B(4) #B(5) #A(6) A#(7) B#(8) #B(9) A#(10) #A(11) #B(12) 

# EXACT SAME STRING PREV:NO



# PASS 1:
NEXT INDEX:1:WITHIN
#A(1) B#(2):RULE:#A B# → #A(1)
NEXT INDEX:2:WITHIN
B#(2) #B(3):RULE:B# #B →
NEXT INDEX:4:WITHIN
#B(4) #B(5):RULE:#B #B → #B(2)
NEXT INDEX:5:WITHIN
#B(5) #A(6):RULE:#B #A → #B(3)
NEXT INDEX:6:WITHIN
#A(6) A#(7):RULE:#A A# → #A(4)
NEXT INDEX:7:WITHIN
A#(7) B#(8):RULE:A# B# → A#(5)
NEXT INDEX:8:WITHIN
B#(8) #B(9):RULE:B# #B →
NEXT INDEX:10:WITHIN
A#(10) #A(11):RULE:A# #A →
NEXT INDEX:12:WITHIN
#B(12):RULE:#B → #B(6)
NEXT INDEX:13:OVERFLOW



# GATHER NEW TOKENS:
#A(1) #B(2) #B(3) #A(4) A#(5) #B(6) 

# EXACT SAME STRING PREV:NO

# PASS 2:
NEXT INDEX:1:WITHIN
#A(1) #B(2):RULE:#A #B → #A(1)
NEXT INDEX:2:WITHIN
#B(2) #B(3):RULE:#B #B → #B(2)
NEXT INDEX:3:WITHIN
#B(3) #A(4):RULE:#B #A → #B(3)
NEXT INDEX:4:WITHIN
#A(4) A#(5):RULE:#A A# → #A(4)
NEXT INDEX:5:WITHIN
A#(5) #B(6):RULE:A# #B → #B(5) A#(6)
NEXT INDEX:7:OVERFLOW



# GATHER NEW TOKENS:
#A(1) #B(2) #B(3) #A(4) #B(5) A#(6) 

# EXACT SAME STRING PREV:NO

# PASS 3:
NEXT INDEX:1:WITHIN
#A(1) #B(2):RULE:#A #B → #A(1)
NEXT INDEX:2:WITHIN
#B(2) #B(3):RULE:#B #B → #B(2)
NEXT INDEX:3:WITHIN
#B(3) #A(4):RULE:#B #A → #B(3)
NEXT INDEX:4:WITHIN
#A(4) #B(5):RULE:#A #B → #A(4)

NEXT INDEX:7:OVERFLOW



# GATHER NEW TOKENS:
#A(1) #B(2) #B(3) #A(4) #B(5) A#(6) 

# EXACT SAME STRING PREV:YES

# Tokens Without Numbers:
#A #B #B #A #B A#

# Solution:
<solution>#A #B #B #A #B A#</solution>
</EXAMPLE 1>
